Summer Session of 1950 
The Summer Session of 1950 will "begin with registration on June 19, and will end with conferring of degrees on August 11. 
RESIDENCE 





RESIDENCE HALL PHONES 
The purpose of the hall extension phones is for the reception of necessary long distance calls to students from family and friends. In order to keep trunk lines open, the operators on the Notre Dame switchboard have been instructed not to put through any local calls on hail extension phones. Instruct your friends locally to call the pay phone number in your hall. Please answer the phones for students * use in your hall. You do your fellow student a service.
